SELECT COUNT(*)
FROM (
    SELECT DISTINCT `t`.`businessCity`
    FROM (
        SELECT `b`.`businessCity`
        FROM `BusinessRegisters` AS `b`
        WHERE `b`.`businessCity` <> ''
        UNION
        SELECT `s`.`City` AS `businessCity`
        FROM `ShopperRegisters` AS `s`
        WHERE `s`.`City` <> ''
    ) AS `t`
) AS `t0`
